Commentary

Providing a Further Explanation for the British Government and Clearly Informing the World

Since British Foreign Secretary Simon delivered his pro-Japanese remarks at the League of Nations General Assembly on the 7th of this month, this newspaper has commented on it twice, deeply regretting his lack of understanding and the fact that it would further exacerbate global disputes. Now, the British government authorities have made a statement, saying that Simon's remarks at the League of Nations General Assembly were intended to promote reconciliation and were not biased towards any party. This expression is indeed sufficient to refresh the ears and eyes of impartial people around the world and dispel their doubts. However, there are still things we cannot help but say, and we would like to provide a further explanation for the British government and clearly inform the world.

The British authorities said: "Britain is a loyal member of the League of Nations and will never lag behind in upholding the dignity of the Covenant." This expression is indeed very firm and bright. But in terms of facts, who was the culprit in undermining the Covenant when the September 18th Incident occurred last year? Even a three-foot-tall child should know. However, a year has passed, and the Northeast Incident has not yet obtained any fair solution in the League of Nations. Every time the League of Nations has a resolution, Japan blatantly violates it, and the League of Nations is intimidated by violence. In order to perfunctorily deceive the world, they have sent an investigation team. Here, we are deeply concerned that the solemn Covenant for maintaining international justice and peace will be torn apart by violence.

This time, the General Assembly has reopened, and the Lytton Commission's report has clearly presented the actual situation of the Northeast Incident to the world. Moreover, Japan's continuous acts of violence over the past year, such as invading Rehe and officially recognizing the puppet organization, are sufficient for the League of Nations to clearly recognize Japan's true colors. In our initial intention, we thought that the Northeast Incident in the League of Nations would finally have a chance to obtain a fair solution this time. Unexpectedly, today's League of Nations is still no different from yesterday's League of Nations. Gathering politicians and diplomats from all over the world in one hall, it still cannot maintain justice and give legitimate sanctions to violence.

Since the investigation team was commissioned by the League of Nations, its report should be trusted by the League of Nations. In this session of the General Assembly, it should especially implement fair trials based on this report. In the report, there are two very definite points in the conclusion on the September 18th Incident: 1) The Japanese military's violence on the night of September 18th cannot be regarded as an act of self-defense. 2) The Manchukuo puppet state cannot be regarded as being produced by a genuine and natural independent movement. If it is not self-defense, it is aggression. If it is not produced by a genuine and natural independent movement, it is monopolized by Japan. The facts are obvious and universally recognized. The League of Nations refuses to make a fair judgment based on the facts recognized in the report, and the British representative Simon, who claims to be a "loyal member" of the League of Nations, publicly expresses pro-Japanese remarks, supporting violence, causing justice to be suppressed and the Covenant to be broken. Therefore, the world's fair-minded people deeply regret the UK and express infinite disappointment with the League of Nations. How can it be strange?

Now that the British authorities have clearly declared their bright attitude, this bright attitude is indeed relied upon by the League of Nations and by world peace. However, we especially hope that the British authorities, in addition to earnestly expressing their bright attitude, will be stricter in demanding correctness in their actions, that is, based on the standpoint of maintaining the Covenant and maintaining peace, make fair suggestions to the General Assembly. Or, they can even adopt the attitude of resolutely invoking Article 15 of the Covenant in the Anglo-Persian oil case, and recommend to the General Assembly, in accordance with Article 15 of the Covenant, effective sanctions against the powerful, so that justice can finally be extended and peace can finally be maintained. Then the British government's upright attitude and spirit will be admired by all fair-minded people around the world.

Secondly, we still dare to say to the British government and to the just people of all countries in the world: Although the Chinese people are now under violent coercion, they firmly believe that violence will never swallow justice and will eventually be subdued by justice. At the same time, they firmly believe that the Chinese nation wants to seek its own independence and freedom for survival, and there is no other way but to rely on self-reliance and self-rescue. The Chinese people earnestly hope that the League of Nations and the just people of the world will rise up together to uphold justice, but they will never rely on the League of Nations, let alone trust any one country. They will rely on self-reliance and self-rescue and maintain the international Covenant, justice, and peace. The Chinese people have now made this determination. Fight on! Violence will eventually be laid to rest at the feet of justice.

Irigoyen, Over Seventy Years Old, Still Has Political Ambition

Bomb Explosion Reveals Conspiracy

Once Ruled the People, Now a Prisoner

Argentina Announces National Emergency Alert

National News Agency, Buenos Aires, 16th - Former Argentine President Irigoyen, once known as the most tyrannical leader in Latin America, was arrested and imprisoned today for plotting to overthrow the government. Irigoyen is now 87 years old, and although old, his ambition has not waned. After being re-elected president in 1928, he still held absolute power, and his cabinet members became mere figureheads. This led to a sudden revolution on February 6, 1930, which resounded throughout the country. Irigoyen was forced to abdicate, but remained in the capital, guaranteeing that he would no longer engage in political activities. However, the government has recently received reports of Irigoyen's activities. With today's bomb case, detectives seized documents and other evidence, discovering that Irigoyen was plotting to overthrow the government. President Uriburu ordered his arrest. The discovery of the conspiracy was due to a bomb explosion today. Police searched and discovered 1,300 bombs hidden in various important places in the capital, preparing to launch an uprising to overthrow the government and seize the army. There was also considerable contact with the provinces, preparing to launch uprisings simultaneously. It was learned that Irigoyen was the mastermind behind this. After the authorities raided various revolutionary agencies in the capital and arrested 50 accomplices, they immediately asked Congress to authorize the government to declare a national emergency alert (i.e., a state of siege, which is slightly less severe than martial law), and urgently ordered secret service personnel to investigate the situation in various provinces to determine whether the military and police were completely reliable.

▲ Reuters, Buenos Aires, 16th - A bomb suddenly exploded at the residence of former President Dr. Irigoyen today. Police went to investigate and discovered thousands of bombs and arrested 15 people. Dr. Irigoyen belongs to the Radical Party. He served as president during the European War, and one of his greatest achievements was keeping Argentina from falling into the war vortex. Dr. Irigoyen tried his best to seek happiness for the laboring class in domestic affairs. The revolution of 1930 occurred, and Dr. Irigoyen left office; otherwise, his term would have lasted until 1934.

▲ Continued Report - Former President Alvear was also arrested. Alvear and Dr. Irigoyen will both be expelled from the country. The cabinet decided to implement a strict plan to maintain order and asked Congress to declare a state of siege. Police were ordered to search the Radical Party headquarters and ordered the newspaper "Public Opinion Freedom" to cease publication. In addition to the bombs, military equipment was also seized at his residence. Police also seized the party's plan, knowing that they planned to capture President Uriburu, occupy various government offices, and use bombs to create terror. Radical Party leaders were clearly involved in this revolutionary conspiracy, and authorities have arrested many people everywhere.

Philippine Authorities Plan to Seize the Livelihood of Overseas Chinese

Schools Add Retail Skills

To Compete with Chinese Merchants

National News Agency, Manila, 17th - The Philippine Department of Education will implement a plan to educate Filipinos in retail skills starting next year to compete with Chinese merchants. Most of the retail businesses in the Philippines are controlled by overseas Chinese. According to statistics from the Bureau of Industry and Commerce, only 18% to 20% of the retail businesses in the entire island are held by Filipinos, while the rest are in the hands of foreigners, with overseas Chinese holding 50% to 60%. Currently, the large stores opened by Filipinos have difficulty competing with Chinese merchants. Therefore, the Philippine authorities have decided to educate the people in the knowledge of retail business. It is temporarily scheduled to add a retail skills course to all secondary schools on the island starting next school year (starting in June next year).

Resolving the War Debt Issue

Hoover is Considering Three Procedures

Plans to No Longer Consult with Roosevelt

National News Agency, Washington, 16th - It is now confirmed that US President Hoover is considering three procedures for resolving the war debt issue. 1. Congress establishes a war debt committee. Hoover still considers this the best of the three options, but he also knows that Congress will oppose the revival of this kind of institution. 2. The existing diplomatic agencies negotiate separately with each debtor nation. If this procedure is adopted, Hoover hopes that each country can submit valuable reports and suggestions so that they can obtain considerable support from Congress in the future. 3. The President himself appoints informal committee members to contact foreign officials on the war debt issue and then make a detailed report on the situation in Europe and the economic situation that will result from continuing the current debt repayment schedule, or the economic consequences of writing off a portion of the debt, so that the President can more easily make special recommendations to Congress. However, regardless of which procedure Hoover chooses, it is heard that he will no longer consult with Roosevelt. Hoover is now trying to resolve this matter before his term expires. If he cannot, it will be transferred to the next president to handle. It is also heard that Hoover is willing to discuss the possibility of amending the agreement for the war debts owed by France, even though they are in default. However, he still does not want to participate in any war debt conference. Yesterday, France, Belgium, Hungary, Estonia, and Poland defaulted on their war debts. Americans were not surprised by this. Today, the Secretary of the Treasury announced that the total amount of these defaults was 14,996,551.85 gold yuan. The total amount paid by Britain, Italy, Czechoslovakia, Finland, Latvia, and Lithuania was 98,685,906.3 gold yuan.

Philippine Independence Bill

Hawes-Cutting Advocates

A Twenty-Year Trial Period

Worse Than George III's Maladministration

National News Agency, Washington, 16th - Today, the US Senate again rejected the amendment by Roussad to allow the Philippines to become independent within eight years, and replaced it with a compromise measure, proposed by the original proponents of the Hawes-Cutting Bill, advocating that the Philippines be allowed to become independent after twelve years. During this transition period, for the first seven years, except for special restrictions on sugar, coconut oil, and ropes, the remaining goods will still be allowed to be imported into the United States duty-free. In the last five years, Philippine goods will be subject to import duties, increasing annually, starting from 5% to 25%. This tax revenue will be used to repay the existing public debt of the Philippines, because Congress firmly insists that the Philippines must repay its public debt and resolve all financial entanglements before starting an independent life. It is now expected that the entire Hawes-Cutting Bill will require several more days of discussion before it can be voted on. The differences between this bill and the Hare-Hawes-Cutting Act passed by the House of Representatives are expected to be easily reconciled in the joint conference committee of the two houses in the future.

▲ Reuters, Manila, 17th - Philippine Senate President Quezon, comparing the US Senate's proposed independence plan for the Philippine Islands with the harsh administration of King George III, convened members of the Philippine legislature today to consider the matter. Quezon said that according to the news received, the US Senate's struggle did not give the Philippines independence, but rather closed the door to America, rejecting Philippine workers and products.

US Democratic Party's Asian Policy (Part 2)

John Hay stated, "For the sake of maintaining the lives of the American people, China is a business and industrial enterprise for Americans. We must demand that its doors be open and that opportunities are equal. We must abolish all differential treatment in American trade with China or in treaties, whether in spheres of influence or in leaseholds in that country, so that we can maintain America's permanent prosperity and increase the welfare of Americans." Since John Hay issued his statement, enlightened people have regarded it as a just argument. Therefore, no matter which party is in power, they will never change this policy. Therefore, the US Asian policy, although seemingly focused on economic aspects, is actually paying close attention to political power.

However, since Japan and Britain are fostering economic power in China, and Japan's political and economic power in China since the Sino-Japanese War has become increasingly unassailable, the US's attempt to expand and foster superior rights in China will have its strong enemy in Japan. Why? Britain's economic power in China has gradually declined after the Opium War, while Japan's has expanded year by year. If the US wants to implement John Hay's policy, it must restrain Japan.

3. The Unchanging US Policy and Facts. As mentioned above, the US Asian policy was originally a policy of suppressing Japan. This policy has been tried to be realized since the time of President Theodore Roosevelt. After the Russo-Japanese War, Roosevelt took it upon himself to mediate. US railroad tycoon Harriman vigorously promoted the management rights of the South Manchurian Railway, but was rejected by Japan. He then collaborated with Britain to establish the Jin-Ai Railway, but was also rejected by Japan and Russia. Later, when the Democratic Party replaced the Republican Party in power (Wilson), the US Far Eastern policy seemed to have changed. However, when the European War broke out in 1914, Japan took Qingdao and occupied all German rights in Shandong under the Anglo-Japanese alliance. The following year, Japan presented the Twenty-One Demands to China, at which point the US rose up in opposition. Later, China participated in the war in the name of the Allied Powers, and the US encouraged the Chinese government to declare all treaties, declarations, and statements between China and Germany invalid to the world. When the European War ended, at the Paris Peace Conference, Japan's important proposals regarding all rights in Qingdao and Shandong Province were rejected. This was all due to President Wilson's machinations. Fortunately, at that time, the Fiume issue caused a conflict between the plenipotentiaries of the US and Italy. The Italian financial tycoon withdrew from the meeting, and the peace conference almost broke down. Fearing that Japan would follow Italy, the US had no choice but to allow Japan's proposal. However, the US's oppression of Japan remained consistently unchanged because the US inherited John Hay's policy and would not stop until it achieved its goal.

4. The Inevitable Fate of Japan and the United States. In 1920, Wilson failed in the election, and Republican Harding succeeded him as president. He convened the Washington Conference, first passing a bill rejecting Japanese immigrants, and then using the London Conference to impose various means of oppression on Japan, isolating Japan. Because of its Asian policy, the facts of the past show that it remains unchanged. However, our people (Japanese) believe that the Democratic Party's victory this time can change its Asian policy. Isn't this just wishful thinking? Today, Japanese often say that Manchuria and Mongolia are Japan's lifeline and are willing to gamble the nation's fate. However, Americans also say that China is America's lifeline and will not allow Japan to dominate it and abandon its century-old plan. Therefore, I say that Japan and the US, separated by the Pacific Ocean, want to compete for this good bait of China, and a war between the two sides will inevitably break out to determine the victor. I hope that the people of our country (Japan) will wake up and not be misled by the fallacies of those who do not understand the general trend of the world. (The End)

Northeast Problem and the League of Nations (4)

Participation of the Investigation Team

Verbal Battle Between Chinese and Japanese Representatives

The signatory nations of the Nine-Power Treaty signed in Washington on February 6, 1922, including Japan, in view of China's need for a transitional period during its reconstruction, jointly agreed to "provide China with the fullest and least obstructed opportunity to develop and maintain for herself an effective and stable government." Unfortunately, one of the greatest difficulties for China in its progress towards unification and construction has been Japan's repeated obstruction of its success. Let's cite one example to illustrate this. Goto Shimpei, a prominent Japanese politician, in his Japanese booklet "Activities of the Japanese People and Army in Manchuria and Mongolia," stated explicitly that when Yuan Shikai was unifying China in the early years of the Republic of China, the Japanese side organized a restoration movement in the three northeastern provinces to overthrow Yuan. The booklet stated directly that Japanese financier Okura Kihachiro provided a large sum of money to Prince Su of the Manchu Qing Dynasty to immediately carry out this movement. Goto also mentioned that Colonel Dohi, commander of the 5th regiment of the Japanese army at the time, was ordered to lead a large number of junior Japanese officers to organize and plan anti-Yuan troops. However, this is a rather old matter, and you may not remember it well. Now, let me present more recent facts to you. In 1927 and 1928, the Japanese government twice dispatched heavy troops to Jinan, the provincial capital of Shandong, ostensibly to protect Japanese residents who were in no danger. In reality, it was to obstruct General Chiang Kai-shek's victorious National Revolutionary Army from unifying North China and bringing it under the control of the Nanjing National Government. On May 28, 1928, the Japanese government, through Prime Minister Tanaka, issued a threatening declaration, stating that if further disturbances occurred in the Beijing and Tianjin areas, Japan would be forced to take appropriate steps to maintain peace and order in the three northeastern provinces. Shortly after this declaration was issued, General Zhang Zuolin was killed in a bomb attack on his train. The purpose of the declaration was also to obstruct the success of China's unification. Subsequently, the Japanese Consul-General in Shenyang, Special Envoy Baron Hayashi, and Japanese Brigade Commander Sato warned General Zhang Xueliang not to contact the Nanjing central government and not to raise the blue sky with a white sun and a field of red flag. On August 9, 1928, General Zhang Xueliang visited Baron Hayashi at the Japanese Consulate-General in response to an invitation and received the same warning. Zhang Xueliang then raised a protest, asking whether this attitude of Japan was reasonable, to which Sato replied, "This is not the time to discuss the reasonableness or unreasonableness of any event. Prime Minister Tanaka has decided that a new flag should not be flown at this time, and that alone is sufficient reason." From the above, it can be seen that Japan, on the one hand, loudly appealed to the world about China's disunity, while on the other hand, insisted on pursuing its policy of obstructing China's unification. This is an extremely strange and meaningful fact, which we must pay attention to. The question for us here is whether Japan sincerely desires China's unification. We can clearly see that Japan deeply fears that after China is unified, Japan's imperial development policy and its hope of conquering the world will be dealt a blow. The Investigation Team's report states on page 13, "From Japan's perspective, the core of the problem lies in its concern about the political development of the new China and its future trends." If we carefully consider the meaning between the lines, we can get its true meaning. The importance of the integrity of any country's organization lies in its impact on the relations of that country with other countries. This impact can often be expressed by many factors, and the development of foreign trade is one of them. In this regard, China's performance is not inferior to that of other countries. In the past 20 years, although countries around the world have developed a perception of China due to a kind of organized and malicious propaganda, China has made a very significant and gradually increasing contribution to the world economy. China's foreign trade statistics are the best tool to refute the accusations of Japanese critics. In 1911, China's total foreign trade was Customs Silver 849,000,000 taels. In 1921, it increased to Customs Silver 1,500,000,000 taels. In 1930, it increased to Customs Silver 2,204,000,000 taels. In other words, China's foreign trade has increased by as much as 158% in the past 20 years. Another reliable indicator of the degree of perfection of a country's political organization is the degree of loyalty and cooperation shown by that country to other countries in respecting international treaties. This cooperation is an indispensable requirement for the realization of a new international life and the organization of world peace. If we use this point as a yardstick, we may ask to what extent has Japan's national organization reached perfection? The real difficulty for the League of Nations at present regarding the incident in the three northeastern provinces is Japan's refusal to respect its international obligations, such as those clearly stipulated in the League of Nations Covenant, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the Nine-Power Treaty, and its refusal to implement its promises to the Administrative Yuan to withdraw Japanese troops stationed in the three northeastern provinces to prevent the severity of the incident from increasing. We will not even ask whether this is due to the unwillingness of the Japanese government or whether it is due to the inability of the Japanese government to control its powerful and influential warlords. Its impact on the world is equally worrying. The League of Nations felt this last year, and today it probably still feels the same way. Regarding this point, if we want to deeply understand the situation in the Far East, we should first understand the purpose and impact of Japan's traditional expansion policy mentioned in the Investigation Team's report. This policy is called the "Continental Policy" by the Japanese, which is a continental policy of conquering Asia. Its steps are divided into two branches: one is North China, which involves invading the three northeastern provinces and North China from Korea, and the other is South China, which involves invading South China, Central China, and various places in the South China Sea, using Taiwan as a base. In the 16th century, Toyotomi Hideyoshi of Japan advocated annexing China. In his letter to the King of Korea, he said:

"People's life in this world has never been more than a hundred years old. How can they live here in depression for a long time? I want to borrow your country's way to cross the mountains and the sea and go straight into the Ming Dynasty, so that its four hundred states will all be transformed into my customs, so as to implement the kingly way for hundreds of millions of years. This is Hideyoshi's long-cherished wish. All those who arrive overseas later will not be released. Your country first sent envoys and coins, and the emperor greatly appreciated it. On the day Hideyoshi enters the Ming Dynasty, he will lead his soldiers to the military camp as my guide."

In the mid-19th century, Kushima, the lord of the Saga domain and the Governor of Hizen, said in his memorial:

"The office of the Shogunete is known as the 'Great General Who Subdues the Eastern Barbarians.' The two characters 'Subduing the Barbarians' are a conspicuous symbol that will never change for all ages. Now that there has been peace for a long time and the morale of the soldiers is lazy, it is precisely the time to take advantage of the situation, display power abroad, and thus be able to reverse the national fortune and establish the national foundation."

Before Saigo Takamori, Okubo Toshimichi advocated annexing Korea and dividing China most vigorously. In his discussion of Japanese policy, he said:

"Japan's greatest hidden danger is Russia. Because of its location, Russia is most likely to obstruct Japan from implementing its continental policy. If Japan is determined to implement this policy, it should immediately form an alliance with Russia and divide the land of China equally."

The reason why I bring up the above sections is not because of their historical interest, but because of their great relevance to Japan's modern policy towards China and the Far East. The spirit contained in the above sections and the policy advocated are no different from Japan's current spirit and policy. On March 31, 1922, the Army and Navy Departments of Tokyo held an important joint meeting, which was attended by the highest-ranking officers of the Army and Navy. A new strategy was decided. The next day, the Tokyo Yomiuri Shimbun reported on the content of the meeting, stating that the highest military advisory body had decided that once a war broke out, Japan should immediately establish a close communication network with the Asian continent from Hankou, Shandong to Harbin, Sakhalin as the first line of defense. Regarding military action plans, the newspaper had the following shocking record: "In order to consolidate its defense line, Japan should first increase the garrison forces in Korea, Sakhalin, and Taiwan, and should use all its strength to obtain the free supply rights of the Hanyang and Pingxiang coal and iron mines, so as to enrich military needs, so that a long-term war can be relied upon, and a final victory can be expected. In order to prepare for the rapid transformation of international relations, Japan should first take Beijing, and at the same time occupy Shenyang and Changchun in the three northeastern provinces, so that there is no need to worry about the lack of supply of various materials."

In the spring of 1922, when the Japanese Diet was in session, Japanese Minister of the Army Yamanashi replied to a question from a member regarding the new military defense plan set by the Supreme Military Conference:

Page 10

"A country that had close contact with Japan in the past (referring to the United Kingdom) has decided not to continue the alliance treaty. Therefore, once a war breaks out, Japan is in danger of being economically blockaded. In order to prevent this situation, Japan should occupy the mainland (referring to China) and Siberia to obtain sufficient food and military supplies."

For hundreds of years, the culmination of the efforts of Japanese soldiers to promote the two-pronged continental development policy, the first step of which is to focus on China as the starting point for conquering all of Asia. Its progress is started simultaneously from the north and the south, just like a scorpion attacking its victim with its head and tail at the same time. Here, we can understand why Japan insisted that China cede the Liaodong Peninsula and the island of Taiwan after the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895. Here, we can deeply understand Japan's seizure of China's Ryukyu Islands in 1879, its occupation of South Manchuria and annexation of Korea after the Russo-Japanese War, its dispatch of troops deep into Hankou in the center of the Yangtze River Basin in 1911, its occupation of Shandong from 1914 to 1922, its presentation of the Twenty-One Demands in 1915, and its hesitation to withdraw the expeditionary force to eastern Siberia, its dispatch of large forces to Jinan in 1927 and 1928, and finally its occupation of Shenyang and other cities on September 18 and 19, 1931, occupying the entire three northeastern provinces, ignoring world opinion, going back on its promises, violating its obligations, and its true meaning of refusing to withdraw its troops. If we measure it by the words of Okubo Toshimichi, we can know the true purpose of the secret treaties repeatedly concluded by the Japanese government with the Russian government in 1907, 1910, 1912, and 1916 to plot to divide Manchuria and Mongolia, and its secret exchange of letters with various countries in 1917 regarding South Manchuria and Shandong Province. And the recent intention of the Japanese government to try to find an allied country among European countries can also be clearly understood. We dare to say that this continental policy, which has been known to the leaders of the new China, is a real threat to peace in the Far East and a major source of unrest for countries around the world. The reason why it is so dangerous is that behind this policy, there is a warlord force that is accustomed to making its own decisions and is unwilling to repent, holding the most powerful war tools, and the method of satisfying its desires is to maintain military force and power everywhere. Although the inevitable unstable state of China during the transitional period should not be unnecessarily prolonged, it itself must not conflict with the new international life based on the rule of law and the principle of resolving disputes peacefully through international methods. Japanese warlords constantly obstruct the unification of China, increase China's difficulties, and use China's various hardships, such as floods and communist disturbances, to promote their land expansion and continental conquest policies. All of these are the real obstacles to peaceful understanding between China and Japan. Looking at the history of Sino-Japanese relations over the past 60 years can prove that my words are not false. Although Japan's continuous wars, military expeditions, and acts of aggression against China over the past 60 years have varied in their time and place of expression, the underlying policy of expansion, occupation, and conquest has continued consistently without any difference. We should pay attention to this policy, the goal of which is not only to acquire Manchuria and Mongolia. According to the memorial of former Japanese Prime Minister Tanaka Giichi, which was often cited by Japanese newspapers before September 1931, and the truthfulness of which was never doubted, controlling China's three northeastern provinces is just one step in conquering the world order. The memorial states:

"If we want to control China in the future, we must first defeat the power of the United States. The meaning of the Russo-Japanese War is largely the same. However if we want to conquer China, we must first conquer Manchuria and Mongolia. If we want to conquer world, we must first conquer China. If China can be completely conquered by our country, other peoples with different customs, such as those in Central Asia, India, and Southeast Asia, will fear and respect us and surrender to us, so that the world will know that East Asia is our East Asia, and will never dare to invade us. This is the legacy of Emperor Meiji, and it is also a necessary matter for the existence of our Japanese Empire."

This plan of Emperor Meiji is still not regarded by Japan as merely an event of historical interest. Judging from the speeches of important Japanese politicians and military personnel today, it seems that the grand strategy of Emperor Meiji is still the guiding force of Japan. Kita Ikki drafted an outline of a Japanese amendment to the legacy law in 1929. After the book was published, it became the bible of general young officers, and it still is today. The book states: "The state has the right to declare and wage war to defend itself or liberate oppressed nations, such as liberating India from the shackles of Britain, or China from the aggression of the great powers." The book also states:

"The state also has the right to wage war against countries that hold a large amount of territory or govern that territory poorly, such as taking Australia from Britain and taking Siberia from Russia." Mori Kaku, the former Chief Cabinet Secretary of Japan, published an article in the Kin'yū Ishi (Gold Stone) Economic Magazine in July of this year, stating that "The Japanese nation is bound by treaties and trapped within its own national borders. If the current interpretation of the Nine-Power Treaty and the Kellogg-Briand Pact is allowed to remain unchanged, Japan will not be able to expand its power in the Far East. If we want to progress, we must break down the defense line of these treaties." The current Minister of the Army, Araki, is already world-famous. In a recent article in the Japanese Army organ magazine Kaikōsha Kiji, he encouraged the Japanese people to be loyal to the national spirit, and also said, "The countries of East Asia are the object of oppression by white people. This is an undeniable fact. Japan should no longer sit idly by and do nothing. The responsibility of the Japanese people lies in opposing all actions of the great powers that are not in accordance with the spirit of the Japanese Empire, because the spirit of the Empire is the embodiment of fairness and justice. Sichuan War Becomes More Chaotic

Twenty Thousand Deaths on Each Side in the Renjia Area

Tian Army Launches Surprise Attack on Liu Wenhui in the Chengdu Area

Unprecedented Bloody Battle in Renjia

Hankou Correspondence: Liu Xiang, the protagonist of the Sichuan War, after occupying Lu Nei and Fuyuan, in order to break up the united front of the Deng, Tian, and Liu factions, personally went to Neijiang to convene a meeting. Tian Songyao, Liu Cunhou, Yang Sen, Li Qixiang, Luo Zezhou, and others all sent representatives to participate. The meeting was held on the 6th, and on the 7th, Liu Xiang issued the third general attack order, with all routes simultaneously mobilizing. The Chengdu battle also broke out again. Liu Wenhui's troops stationed in Chengdu numbered more than ten brigades, with troop strength doubling that of the Tian army. They were originally in a position of certainty to win. Because Deng Xihou mediated, Liu was also unwilling to break with Tian and was eager to resist the Chongqing army, so he abandoned Chengdu on the 9th, allowing the Tian army to garrison it. His troops were concentrated in the Xinjin, Chongqing, Wenjiang, Shuangliu, Renshou, Qingshen, Jiading, and Jingyan areas. It is said that there are still about 50,000 to 60,000 men in strength. Together with the Chen Hongwen and Chen Shunong factions, there are about 70,000 to 80,000 men. Although the two Chens had been assigned back to Deng Xihou's control, it did not become a reality. Therefore, although they retreated to a corner, they did not show weakness. Liu Xiang, seeing that Chengdu was exclusively occupied by the Tian army, wanted to take advantage of the situation to eliminate the 24th Army. Therefore, he dispatched the Tang Shizun, Pan Wenhua, and Wang Zhiyi divisions with lightning speed and advanced rapidly, with one army attacking Jiading as the left route, one army attacking Jingyan as the middle route, and one army attacking Renshou as the right route. Liu Xiang himself was stationed in Longchang, commanding and coordinating. The 24th Army also divided into three routes to meet the enemy. Liu Wenhui withdrew from Chengdu on the 9th and went to Jiading in person. The Chongqing army launched a general attack on the 7th, and until the 9th, it only engaged in guerrilla warfare with the provincial army and did not distinguish between victory and defeat. On the 10th, Liu Wenhui arrived in Jiading, and the battle suddenly became fierce. From the 10th to the 12th, there was a bloody battle for three days and nights. The lines of Jingyan and Renshou did not change much. On the Jiading line, the provincial army won. Liu Xiang heard the news in Longchang and urgently dispatched reinforcements. From the 14th, he launched a counterattack, and until dawn on the 16th, there was another bloody battle for two days and two nights. Including the previous battles, there were a total of five days and five nights. Neither side rested, and the number of soldiers killed reached more than 20,000. The number of wounded was not included, and the number of civilians killed and injured was also large. In the Sichuan War over the years, the sacrifice was the greatest in this battle. Liu Xiang, because the left route was frustrated, in addition to dispatching reinforcements, urgently telegraphed Tian Songyao to send troops to attack his rear route. Tian, having exclusively occupied Chengdu, had already achieved his goal. However, because he and Liu Xiang touted cooperation, he also divided his troops into three routes and advanced towards Liu Wenhui's defense area. The 1st Division, Zeng Nanfu, and the 2nd Route, He Deyu, were assigned to the left route and advanced towards Renshou's Jitianpu. The 3rd Division, Luo Bochang, and the 1st Route, Liu Hanxiong, were assigned to the middle route and advanced towards Shuangliu. The 1st Division, Dong Changan, and the 28th Army, Huang Yin, were assigned to the right route and advanced towards Wenjiang and Chongqing, echoing Liu Xiang's troops from afar. Among them, the Huang Yin Division was under Deng Xihou's command. Although Deng was stationed in Chengdu, he did not help the Tian army attack the 24th Army. This time, Huang's division set out without Deng's order, which was his personal free action. The system of the Sichuan army is chaotic, and discipline is lost. Such cases are countless. It is difficult for Liu Wenhui to take care of all parties with the strength of one army. However, since his defense line has been shortened, and his troops have been concentrated, all the generals and soldiers, with their survival at stake, are willing to fight to the death. If they win, they can still sweep through Chengdu and restore Lu Nei. If they lose, they can still retreat to Yaan, make a comeback. Therefore, from the current situation, if Liu Xiang expresses his withdrawal early, obeys the orders of the central government, and forces Liu Wenhui to step down under certain conditions, the 24th Army may disintegrate invisibly. If he is too hasty, their unity will be stronger. The conclusion of the Sichuan War is still unknown. (December 16)

Second Street Battle in Chengdu

Chongqing Correspondence: Chengdu was originally garrisoned by the Liu Wenhui, Tian Songyao, and Deng Xihou factions. However, the Tian faction recently took advantage of the fact that Liu's troops were battling Liu Xiang's troops in the Yizhou area and suddenly attacked Liu's troops stationed in Chengdu. As a result, the Tian army collapsed and withdrew from Chengdu and lost the arsenal. Then Deng Xihou came forward to make peace, using the unity of the Baoding clique as a cover, and convened a three-army cooperation meeting. At that time, the Tian army had just been defeated, and its vigor had not recovered, so it naturally admitted defeat. Liu Wenhui thought that after contacting the Deng and Tian armies, he could deal with the 20th Army with all his strength. Therefore, he first held a three-army peace conference in Tianhui Town (30 li away from Chengdu), and then further held a five-army cooperation meeting in Chengdu. Participants included Liu Zhaogan, the commander of the 1st Division of the Sichuan Shaanxi Army; representatives Fu Jianwu and Su Mou; Qiao Zhongquan, Wang Weizi, and Liu Jafan, the commanders of the 20th Army; Liu Wenhui, Xiang Yuren, Leng Yindong, and Wu Jingbo, the commanders of the 24th Army; Deng Xihou, Yang Xiuchun, Ma Dezai, and Huang Yin, the commanders of the 28th Army; and Sun Zhen, Dong Changan, Luo Bochang, and Wang Mingzhang, the commanders of the 29th Army. The resolutions are as follows: (1) The five armies should act in unison, cooperate thoroughly, and form an alliance to attack and defend. However, in order to maintain the dilapidated situation, they should adhere to the principle of "I will not attack if others do not attack me." (2) The finances of the five divisions should be open, and the stationing should be averaged according to the circumstances. Efforts should be made to supplement them. (3) The five divisions should be stationed together in Chengdu and telegraph Liu Xiang to open up Chongqing and Wanxian, break the defense zone system, and withdraw from all counties occupied by the 24th Army, which should be handled by the five armies. Therefore, at that time, the voice of cooperation among the five divisions rose to the clouds, and the Sichuan Political Consolidation Committee was also established in Chengdu. Ten members were elected, including Sun Decao and Ma Yaosheng (29th Army), Wu Jingbo and Xiang Yuren (24th Army), Wang Weizi and Qiao Zhongquan (20th Army), representative Su and Fu Jianwu (Sichuan Shaanxi Army), Wen Mengtao and Yang Xiuchun (28th Army). Unexpectedly, at noon on the 10th, the Tian army suddenly took advantage of the 24th Army's unpreparedness, and Sun Decao led the Luo Bochang and Zeng Xiantong divisions to launch a fierce attack on Chengdu. The Chengdu guard brigade of the 24th Army, led by Shi Zhaohuo, was defeated. At the same time, fierce fighting broke out at the southeast gates. Street battles also broke out in the city's Jiangjun Street and other places. The 24th Army set fire to civilian houses on Wenmiao West Street. Finally, because reinforcements did not arrive, Shi's division withdrew from Chengdu on the night of the 12th and camped at Xinjin, Shuangliu, and the outer east arsenal, preparing for a counterattack. On the 13th, Sun led 3 regiments to attack the arsenal, and fierce fighting broke out again. As for Liu Wenhui himself, he is currently stationed in Meishan, and the military headquarters is also located in Meishan. The provincial government plans to move from Chengdu to Meishan in the next few days. All the 24th Army troops, such as Chen Mingqian, Zhang Deping, Chen Hongwen, Leng Yindong, Peng Han, Yu Lie, Liu Wencai, and Li Yushu, are stationed in Jiading, Qionglai, Jiajiang, Pengshan, Jingyan, Meishan, and Renshou, with a troop strength of about 60 regiments. On the afternoon of the 14th, the Chengdu battle had stopped, and Deng Xihou came forward to mediate again. The 24th Army ceded the arsenal to the 29th Army, and the Tian army also stopped military action. However, it is unknown whether Tian and Liu can get along to the end. (December 5)

Liu Zhennian's Division is About to Arrive in Fujian

Liu Expresses Obedience to the Fujian Authorities

Fuzhou Correspondence: The 21st Division of Liu Zhennian has been transferred from Jiaodong to the border between Fujian and Zhejiang. The second brigade of the division's first batch, led by Liang Lizhu, arrived at the border between Fujian and Zhejiang on the 5th. The advance troops have advanced to the two counties of Pucheng and Zhenghe. The artillery, engineering, and baggage regiments and battalions of the second batch also arrived in Lishui and Longquan on the 7th and continued to advance. On the 9th, the provincial government received a telegram from Sun Yi, the magistrate of Pucheng County, stating, "Liu's division will arrive in Pu soon. It has been found that Zhejiang Province has a heavy burden of entertainment, and Lu banknotes are not in general circulation. The county of Zhi has been devastated after the disaster, and there is no way to raise military expenses. The military needs of the Qian brigade (i.e., the provincial defense army Qian Yuguang brigade) are particularly urgent these days. How should it be handled? Please telegraph instructions immediately." The provincial government, considering that county governments have recently been making excuses for handling military expenses, and have been advancing funds without permission, telegraphed the county magistrate, requiring him to report the arrival of Liu's troops in advance and not to advance funds without authorization. As for the supply of the Qian brigade, it will be raised separately. Furthermore, Liu Zhennian, considering that it was necessary to contact the provincial authorities as his troops would arrive in Fujian soon, specially sent Colonel Han Meicen, a counselor, to Fujian on the 11th to state to the provincial government and the Pacification Commissioner that his troops were coming to Fujian to suppress bandits in accordance with the order, would absolutely obey the command and dispatch of the authorities, and would cooperate effectively with various troops. However, most of the officers and soldiers of the division are from the north, and they are new to the south, and there are inevitably differences in customs and language. It is hoped that guidance will be given. (December 12)

The Inspection Group from Beiping, Nanjing, and Shanghai Returns to Hankou

Land Barren and Desolate, A Heartrending Sight

Numerous Disaster Victims Urgently Awaiting Relief

Hankou Communication: The inspection group from Beiping, Nanjing, and Shanghai, having departed from Hankou a few days ago to inspect the central Hubei region, passing through Yingcheng, Zaoshi, Tianmen, Yuekou, Zhangjiegang, Shayang, Jingzhou, Shashi Xindi, and entering Honghu, Xiaoshakou, Qujiawan, Fengkou, and Xiaogang, returned to Xindi on the 15th. Additionally, the Wuhan community's new inspection group for the recovered bandit areas also inspected the central Hubei region, passing through Yingcheng, Hanchuan, Tianmen, Qianjiang, Mianyang, and Jianli counties, arriving at Xindi from Fengkou on the 13th. After the inspection groups gathered in Xindi, they separately boarded steamships and returned to Hankou. The three inspection groups from Beiping, Nanjing, and Shanghai boarded the Sanjiang ship together, while the Wuhan inspection group traveled on the Taifeng ship alone. On the 16th at 6 PM, everyone arrived in Hankou. According to the observations made by a member of the group, the following points were noted: (1) The people's livelihood is dire. Houses are dilapidated, and land is barren everywhere. Residents in the cities eat grains, water chestnuts, wild water chestnuts, and other things. Farmers in the villages dig up wild grasses to eat and steam flour from water chestnuts and wild water chestnuts to make steamed buns to stave off hunger. The tragic situation is heartrending. Mianyang County is the most devastated, with approximately eight-tenths of the houses destroyed, half by bandits and half by soldiers. There is a lack of oxen, farming tools, and seeds everywhere. (2) Communist Party remnants are lurking. Although the main forces of the Communist bandits have been suppressed everywhere, remnants inevitably remain in hiding. A large number of Communist Party members have surrendered themselves. If no measures are taken to provide relief to the disaster victims, public security will be greatly threatened. (3) The Honghu Dike. This dike is where the lives and property of the people of Mianyang, Jianli, and Qianjiang counties are entrusted. It has not been repaired for several years, and much of it has collapsed, urgently requiring repair. (4) Local Order. Public security in various places is maintained by the Tenth Army. There are also organizations of defense corps and anti-Communist volunteer armies. Order is very stable, and displaced people are returning one after another. (5) Military Discipline. In the past, the discipline of the stationed troops was often poor, and there were reports of various acts of oppression against the people. The troops of the Tenth Army currently stationed have relatively strict discipline and have good relations with the people. (December 16th)

Songjiang

Confessions of Bank Robbers

After the suspects in the Songjiang branch robbery of the Xingye Bank, Niu Jinpu and others, were escorted back to Songjiang, the county Public Security Bureau conducted an interrogation. The confessions of informants and suspects are summarized below: (1) Jin Yunxiu's confession: 36 years old, from Quanjiao County, Anhui, doing small business. In early September, I met Tong Liwen and an unknown person at the small vegetable market in the French Concession. Tong introduced Sun Haiquan to my house for dinner. The second time, we went to a teahouse for tea. Tong asked me who had money, and when I didn't answer, they scolded me for not being a good friend. Sun said that they even dared to rob the Songjiang bank, so why should they be afraid of this? Later, they robbed No. 8, Meihua Lane, on Avenue Joffre in the French Concession. I was afraid of being falsely accused, so I reported it to the police. After Niu Jinpu was arrested, Zheng Shaobo and Li Yinghan were arrested at Sun Haiquan's house. (1) Qian Kaijun, 38 years old, from Chaoxian County, Anhui. I have a relative, Ma Chaoding, who is a messenger in the Special Service Company of the Independent Brigade of the 88th Division, stationed in Songjiang. After working with Niu, I heard Ma Chaojun say that the Xingye Bank robbery was done by Niu Jinpu and others. After the bank robbery, Niu lived in a Western-style house in Wende Lane on Avenue Joffre and married a Cantonese actress for 800 yuan, but ran away in less than a week. Liu Zhiqing guarded the back door when Niu committed this crime, and Niu Jinpu guarded the Longmen. Now, Ji Yiming has been sentenced to four years and six months in Shanghai for robbing him. If this person can be caught, the case can be clarified. (1) Niu Guo's confession: from Hefei, Anhui. The Xingye robbery was done by Liu Tanqing, Ji Yiming, Chen Penghai, and others. On the 22nd day of the fifth lunar month, they divided the spoils at my house, 1,600 yuan per share. Ji, Wu, and Chen each received two shares because they had pistols, and my husband, Jinpu, received one share. Because I had a quarrel with my husband, he gave me 600 yuan. I went back to Hefei with Sun Haiquan, but the boat was robbed at Huoxikou. I returned to Shanghai, etc. (1) Niu Jinpu was a lieutenant platoon leader in the 88th Division. The Xingye robbery was robbed by Liu Zhiqing, Ji Yiming, Wu Dawei, and Chen Penghai. I put the money and tickets in a rattan basket, and I got 1,500 yuan. I told my wife to take 600 yuan back to Hefei. Now Ji Yiming has been arrested on Avenue Edouard and sentenced to four years and six months of imprisonment. The money I got has been gradually spent. (1) Ying Han and Zheng Shaobo confessed together that they had been soldiers in the 88th Division and were dismissed. They were doing small business in Shanghai. This time, I went to Sun Haiquan's place to see, but I was arrested in the bank robbery, which had nothing to do with me. (1) Shao's confession: I know Sun Haiquan, but I really don't know about the robbery. (1) Sun Haiquan's confession: I used to be a soldier in the 88th Division, first teacher Niu Jinpu, I got 1,600 yuan from the bank robbery, and then I ordered the teacher's wife to return to Anhui with me. After encountering robbers at Huoxikou and robbing the rattan basket of banknotes, I returned to Shanghai. Now Ji Yiming has been sentenced in Shanghai and is still appealing, so he has not been brought back. The county Public Security Bureau has escorted the suspects to the procuratorate for investigation and prosecution.

Jiading

Agricultural Bank's Measures to Relieve Farmers

The Farmers Bank of the Seventh District of this county, because of the local famine and after the war, the farmers' economy is full of holes and sores. The value of cotton and rice is low. If they are sold at a low price, the loss will be great. Therefore, it specially handles mortgage loans for agricultural products. Any farmer who wants to borrow money from the bank only needs to unite 10 to 30 people to form a credit production association, provide a guarantee, and ask the township head and district head to prove it. Rice and cotton can be used as collateral for loans. White rice is mortgaged for five yuan per stone, and cotton is mortgaged for ten yuan per dan. The interest rate is 9.8% per month. In addition, the mortgaged goods do not need to be deposited in the bank, but only need to be stored in the office of the director of the credit production association, which is jointly responsible for safekeeping by the director of the association. The procedures are simple and convenient for farmers.

Wuxi

Party Headquarters Thoroughly Investigates District Chief's Accusation

The county party headquarters held its 51st committee meeting yesterday, chaired by Xu Yongji. The following is a summary of the key cases resolved: (1) Committee member Gui Wochen reported that he was appointed to investigate the situation of Li Yaoting and others successively accusing the fifth district chief Zhu Chenghong of electoral fraud and covering up property grabbing and destroying evidence. He should write to the county government for investigation. (2) Guangqin Fifth Branch Road Qingfeng Yarn Factory's illegal construction destroyed the road. A letter should be sent to the county government to instruct the Construction Bureau to handle it. (3) Responding to the Shanghai County Party Headquarters, a telegram was sent to the central government to quickly correct the abolition of the Industry Department in Jiangsu Province.

New Measures to Relieve Farmers

The Farmers Bank, in order to relieve farmers from low grain prices and circulate the rural economy, opened public warehouses to lend and mortgage agricultural products. Warehouses have been set up in five places in the countryside. However, recently, in order to provide universal relief and enable farmers to benefit, special changes have been made to the measures, changing to a limit of 40 stones of white rice per person, with a limit of 200 silver dollars. Farmers can fill in the certificates themselves without the need for others to guarantee them. However, according to regulations, paddy rice and brown rice cannot be mortgaged. The Anzhen storage warehouse has been repeatedly requested by local people, and it has been agreed to discount the market value. The Farmers Bank has approved the change and will implement it soon.

Baitangwei Almost Becomes a Den of Thieves

Baitangwei in the northern countryside borders the Tianshang, Wan'an, and Qingcheng districts. The river surface is vast and the land is remote. It has always been a den of bandits. Later, the water police district sent patrol boats to station there, and it was slightly calmed down. Since the reform of the water police system in the 16th year of the Republic of China, the garrison has been cancelled. Robberies have been frequent in recent years, and few have been solved. Since autumn this year, there have been no less than 20 robberies of boats and flights. Travelers all regard it as a fearful place. A few days ago, a farmer surnamed Li from Yangjiawei hired a boat to return rent rice to the city. While passing through it, four bandits opened fire and robbed him, taking away clothes, rice, and foreign money worth about 40 yuan. In addition, a guest from Doumen, surnamed Hong, and a farmer surnamed Cai from Taixiang were also robbed in the dike. Because the losses were still small, they did not report to the county.

Zhenjiang

Disputes Arise from Jealousy Among Competitors

Recently, Tiantian Store in Shanxiang, this port, has been transporting and selling silk cloth parts, adhering to the principle of small profits, and for a time, customers gathered and the door was crowded. Because of the development of its business, it was envied by the Taiyuanchang Cloth Store next door, so it also held a big sale, posted slogans, and promoted it vigorously. Cloth stalls were set up on the street next to the store, and the shop assistants were sent out to shout loudly, attracting the attention of passers-by. At about 5:00 p.m. yesterday, the two stores clashed because of jealousy. The employees of the two stores each defended one side and staged a martial arts drama. The two shop assistants of Taiyuanchang threw the cloth stalls and the cloth pieces on the counter of Tiantian Store on the ground. For a time, pedestrians stopped, and the viewers blocked the road, and traffic was cut off. Later, the police of the section brought all the shop assistants of both sides to the second branch of the third bureau. It is reported that the owner of Taiyuanchang, Jin Nuoyan, died suddenly at 1:00 a.m. this morning because of his anger.

The Nantong Public Funds and Public Property Management Office previously issued loan coupons of 50,000 yuan due to local financial shortage. It is now processing the payment of interest and principal and will be completed within the year.

Demobilization of the Security Regiment

The security regiments in various districts of Nantong have been recruited and trained, but due to the shortage of pay, there have been constant twists and turns. The county government has now received an order from the province to demobilize the recruits and recruit from each household. Training will begin on January 1 next year.

Four-Year-Old Girl Dies in a Kiln Fire

There is a house in the backyard of the Yida Qianzhuang on Zuowei Street in this city, which is leased to the manager of Dafu Company, Nanpu, the president of the Bank of Communications, Jiang Xuanpu, and the shareholder of the Zhuang, Ye Qixian. Ye has two daughters, one four years old and one one year old. Ye's four-year-old daughter was burned to death because she did not escape in time. The nanny was severely burned, and the president of Jiang was injured in the head. The losses were huge.

Since the Provincial Highway Bureau temporarily designated Caizhuang Port in Zhapu as a shelter area and started surveying, no one has paid attention to the barren mountains, and the value has soared suddenly. Shanghai real estate agents have entrusted people to purchase them. Some time ago, it was rumored that Hangzhou Mayor Zhao Zhiyou also bought a large number of them. Bandit Den Cracked, Ransom Rescued

The police of the Seventh Branch of the Shaoxing Public Security Bureau, together with the Linpu Water Police Team, the County Basic Team, and the police of the Zhuji Public Security Bureau, yesterday co-operated in hunting down the bandits involved in the kidnapping of Tu Zubei in the Siguazhan Liangting area. Compatriots Arise Quickly!

Help Wang Delin Who Is Bitterly Fighting Against Japanese Aggression

The Lofty Spirit of Killing Enemies, Unyielding and Unyielding

Scolding Thieves Relieves Pain, Laudable and Moving

General Zhu Sends Representatives to Shanghai to Beg for Assistance

The Shanghai Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association received a letter from Liang Yuanshan and Zhang Chuyu, representatives of Wang Delin, yesterday, enclosing a copy of an urgent telegram from Dongning, and requesting assistance.

It is up to our compatriots across the country to make practical arrangements and not delay any longer. The war situation in the next few days will be continuously reported."

The troops have more than 70,000 people, and the clothing and supplies are extremely difficult. Commander Wang has been raising funds on his own and with donations from all parties to barely support them until today. More than half of the officers lack winter clothes, weaving grass into shoes, and folding quilts into clothes. The plight is indescribable. The army is located in the key hub of the three provinces, and the relationship is extremely important. After the Soviet army's defeat, the defense area has become even more tense. It is urgent to find a way to provide relief to avoid being taken advantage of by the enemy. It is now planned to calculate based on 30,000 people, with each person's clothing, hats, shoes, socks, and other expenses costing seven yuan, totaling 210,000 yuan. This is the lowest limit. Please find a way to raise funds and issue them in advance. The matter is of utmost importance. I specially sent Wang Delin's representative Liang Detang to come forward to ask for instructions and report everything. Please contact and handle it. I can't help but pray, etc.

Song Qingling and Others Initiate the China League for Civil Rights

Song Qingling, Cai Yuanpei, Yang Quan, Li Zhaohuan, Lin Yutang, and others initiated the organization of the China League for Civil Rights, and issued a declaration, saying, "It is most regrettable that the civil rights demanded by the Chinese people with revolutionary sacrifices have not yet been realized. Records of suppressing public opinion and illegal arrests and killings are almost commonplace in newspapers. Even young men and women are sometimes suspected of being political prisoners and are subjected to secret military trials. Even the minimum human right of public trial to seek civil rights defense from social public opinion is deprived. We deeply know that to effectively and fully reform this state, we must strive to transform the environment that produces this state. However, we also know that all advanced countries have world organizations to protect civil rights, led by Einstein, Gide, Dewey, Russell, and Rolland. The main purpose of this organization is to protect the freedom of thought and social freedom necessary for human life and social evolution. For the same reason, we propose the organization of the China League for Civil Rights. The purpose of this league is: (1) To fight for the release of domestic political prisoners and the abolition of illegal detention, torture, and killings. This league is willing to first devote itself to the majority of nameless and socially unnoticed prisoners. (2) To provide domestic political prisoners with legal and other assistance, and to investigate prison conditions and publish facts about domestic oppression of civil rights in order to arouse social public opinion. (3) To assist all struggles for freedom of association, assembly, speech, press, and other civil rights. This league will establish a national committee, which will be chaired by an executive committee of five to seven people. The national committee will be composed of two representatives elected by each branch. It will meet once a year to elect executive committee members and discuss league affairs. The executive committee will serve for a term of one year and will have a chairman and several secretaries. This league will establish a general headquarters in Shanghai and branches in major cities in the country. Each branch will meet at least once a month. The branch representatives of the national committee will report the branch's situation to the executive committee every month. Anyone who agrees with the league's propositions and is willing to engage in the practical work of realizing these propositions, regardless of nationality, gender, or political beliefs, may become a member of this league upon introduction by three members and approval by a majority of the executive committee. The executive committee may refuse to join the league to candidate members who have participated in the past in acts of depriving civil rights. The membership fee of this league is three yuan per year for individual members and ten yuan per year for group members, and donations may be raised to maintain league affairs. Preparatory Committee of the China League for Civil Rights: Song Qingling, Cai Yuanpei, Yang Quan, Li Zhaohuan, Lin Yutang, et al.

China League for Civil Rights

Telegram for the Rescue of Xu Deheng and Others

The China League for Civil Rights sent a telegram to the authorities in Beiping and Nanjing, saying, "Mr. Chiang Kai-shek, Standing Committee Member of the Central Political Conference in Nanjing, Mr. Song Ziwen, Acting President of the Executive Yuan, and Mr. Yu Xuezhong, Commander of the Beiping-Tianjin Garrison, with respect. Reports state that police detectives in Beiping illegally arrested and imprisoned professors and students from various schools, including Xu Deheng and others, and have not released them to this day. This is the worst kind of destruction of the rule of law and trampling on civil rights. In recent years, the national situation has declined, and the morale of the people has been depressed, all because civil rights have not been established. When people are at home, they are afraid of not being able to guarantee their lives. How can they inspire the spirit of fighting against the enemy? If we want the whole country to unite sincerely and face the national crisis together, the government must immediately issue an order to the whole country to protect the people's freedom of assembly, association, speech, publication, and belief, strictly prohibit the illegal detention of people and the censorship of news, and immediately release the teachers and students of schools illegally detained in Beiping, including Xu Deheng, in order to value civil rights and promote justice. Song Qingling, Cai Yuanpei, Yang Quan, Li Zhaohuan, Lin Yutang, and others, Preparatory Committee of the China League for Civil Rights, jointly launched on December 17th.

National Joint Association for National Salvation

Yesterday's Celebration of the Resumption of Diplomatic Relations Between China and the Soviet Union

The National Goods Association Sends Telegram to Thank Soviet Russia

The National Joint Association of National Salvation Groups held a celebration meeting at 9:00 a.m. yesterday for the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and the Soviet Union. More than 200 people attended, including Long Xiangsan, Zhang Junguang, Tu Liang, Zuo Hua, Chen Zhenquan, and Ma Zhiying. Zhang Junguang was elected chairman. After the ceremony, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting. Then, Tu Liang, the secretary-general of the association, explained the significance of the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and the Soviet Union. Then, it was unanimously resolved to send a telegram to Soviet Russia to express their joy. The meeting ended at about 11:00 a.m. The telegram to the Soviet Union is recorded as follows: "To the Soviet Russian government and all the Russian people in Moscow, with respect. Unfortunately, our country has been invaded and massacred by Japanese imperialism. Since the September 18th Incident last year and the January 28th Incident this year, our entire Chinese people have been risking their lives to fight against Japan every day. However, in this difficult environment, seeking liberation is no easy task. Your country is a revolutionary country and takes helping small and weak nations as its responsibility. You should have deep sympathy for our country's misfortune. This time, the Japanese imperialists forcibly occupied our three northeastern provinces, and those who suffered the most have been clearly revealed, and the disadvantage to your country is also an undeniable fact. Therefore, China and Russia are countries that share weal and woe. If we want to ensure peace in East Asia and the survival of both countries, we must unite and fight together. We are grateful for the preferential treatment given to General Su Bingwen. From the beginning of the establishment of our association, we advocated restoring diplomatic relations between China and the Soviet Union and working together for justice to eliminate violence. Now that the governments of the two countries have officially announced the resumption of diplomatic relations, our association is overjoyed to hear this and held a celebration meeting. We hope that your country and the people will treat each other with sincerity and unite closely and fight together with us. The future of both countries will benefit from this."

The Joint Association of National Goods Factories in this city also sent a telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing, requesting them to convey it to the Soviet Russian government in Moscow to express their gratitude. The original text is as follows: (Omitted above) "This time, General Su Bingwen of our country worked hard to resist Japan, but retreated into your territory due to lack of ammunition and support. The Japanese are insidious and treacherous and demanded extradition. Your country has strictly adhered to neutrality and upheld justice, which is a sign of great public spirit. As the resumption of diplomatic relations is just beginning, we hope to send ambassadors to each other to negotiate treaties and resolve county cases, so that the two major countries on the west coast of the Pacific Ocean can enhance friendship and maintain peace forever. Special telegram to express our gratitude. Please approve. Shanghai National Goods Factory Joint Association."

Volunteer Army Support Association Sends Telegrams to the Chinese and Soviet Governments

Regarding the Expression of Sino-Russian Re-establishment of Diplomatic Relations

Fully Opening a New Era of Automatic Diplomacy, a Bright Future is Emerging, Real Peace on the West Coast of the Pacific, Both Nations Can Shoulder the Mission. Since the re-establishment of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, the national public has expressed sympathy. Yesterday, the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association of this city sent a telegram to the central government to express its gratification, and also telegraphed the Soviet Russian government, hoping to work together in the spirit of equality and mutual assistance. The two telegrams are recorded separately below:

(Telegram to the National Government) Respectfully to the Nanjing National Government Executive Yuan Ministry of Foreign Affairs: Our country's diplomacy has always been observing the intentions of the great powers and has been unable to act independently, often delaying and making mistakes, causing endless harm. In the past, due to policy relations, diplomatic relations between China and Russia were severed, resulting in isolation and lack of assistance. The current national crisis of strong neighbors pressing the border began with this. This time, the government authorities clearly distinguished the relationship between international enemies and friends, established new diplomatic rules, resolutely restored the old good relations, and the great powers were stunned on the day of the announcement, and the whole country sympathized. This is the measure that our independent Republic of China should have, and it is also enough to open a new era of self-persuasion diplomacy. Our association is determined to assist the Northeast Volunteer Army. For half a year, we have deeply understood the difficult situation of the Volunteer Army. It is difficult to find complete success without transforming the environment.

Fortunately, we have this good opportunity now, and a bright future has emerged. It is easier to struggle and achieve results. It is hoped that the government authorities will consider the more than 30 million dying compatriots and the 4 million miles of lost territory, and quickly determine a self-help policy to respond to this newly created environment. We respectfully telegraph our gratification and look forward to working hard for the country. Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, Standing Directors: Chu Fucheng, Li Cishan, Yin Zhufu, Wu Shan, Feng Shaoshan, Yu Huanzheng, Yan Zhifang, Li Shaochuan, Chen Yafu, etc. kowtow together.

(Telegram to the Soviet Russian Government) Respectfully to the Russian Embassy in Beiping for translation and transfer to the Soviet Russian Government: China and the Soviet Union are neighbors and have always maintained friendly relations. Unfortunately, in the past, diplomatic relations were interrupted, but not only did commercial relations between the people not stop, but they continued to progress. Your country has completed the Five-Year Plan with the spirit of revolutionary construction. In today's world economic recession, it is uniquely able to manage with ease and is not controlled by the environment. Looking around the world, our admiration is extreme. Recently, General Su Bingwen led his troops to retreat into your country, and you have graciously accommodated and treated them favorably. You have also held firm to justice and rejected Japan's unreasonable demands, which is deeply appreciated. This time, our two governments resolutely restored diplomatic relations and exchanged envoys, and our people are inexplicably gratified. From now on, the two trades will surely make rapid progress, and the benefits to the people of both countries will be endless. Moreover, your country's completed national economic construction is enough to help our country learn from others. To seek the welfare of the people, we can go by different paths and achieve the same goal. We also hope that our two great nations will work together in the spirit of equality and mutual assistance to strive for the peace and order of the Far East. We firmly believe that the actual peace on the west coast of the Pacific can only be shouldered by our two countries, China and the Soviet Union. We hereby send this telegram to express our thoughts and respectfully wish all the people of your country boundless happiness. Republic of China Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, Standing Directors: Chu Fucheng, Li Cishan, Yin Zhufu, Wu Shan, Feng Shaoshan, Yu Huanzheng, Yan Zhifang, Li Shaochuan, Chen Yafu, kowtow together.
