Amateur Random Talks

The Psychology of Worry and Depression

— Pu

In the last issue's "Casual Talk," we felt inspired by the generally poor living environment and wanted to find a positive way out to break the current state of depression. We believed that since everyone suffered the same oppression, the liberation from this oppression could not be achieved by the efforts of one or two people alone. Therefore, we suggested that we should first start with organized research, discuss various strategies that require joint efforts to transform the situation, and make practical attempts as soon as there are some results. However, in the past five or six days, we have received many letters from readers. On the one hand, they acknowledge the necessity for like-minded shop assistants and apprentices to unite, but on the other hand, they still feel that the future of such uncertain unity is extremely bleak. The words are filled with tones of worry and depression. This kind of depressed psychology is too important, and it is very necessary to bring it up for discussion seriously.

We should deeply understand that in the current situation where foreign enemies have already entered our homes and the domestic politics are still extremely chaotic, and the people's livelihood is extremely poor, the so-called worry and depression are actually a natural result. It is a kind of feeling that any thoughtful young person should have. Otherwise, what difference is there between them and a group of people who live in a drunken dream, have no feeling for the survival of the country and the nation, and live like parasites? However, we should recognize that worry is different from pessimism. Pessimism is the result of discouragement, while worry arises from dissatisfaction with the status quo and implies a consciousness of seeking a way out. Therefore, worry can also be said to be the vanguard of transforming the status quo. Every improvement in the status quo can be said to be the result of efforts made after each period of worry, that is, a kind of true, supreme happiness after worry. However, what we must pay close attention to is that after worry and depression, people often easily fall into pessimism, corruption, and a lack of motivation. Those who can actively struggle after worry and do not enter a path of negativity and decadence can only be achieved by those with considerable knowledge and perseverance.

Therefore, here, we must clearly recognize that the great path to resolving worry is the pursuit of knowledge and the cultivation of a spirit of struggle. It requires effort to achieve. The broader and more complex the problem of worry, the more knowledge is needed, and the slower the progress will be. We should have perseverance, gather like-minded people, and work together. Only with "where there is a will, there is a way" can we solve this worry one day. The happiness of a successful endeavor after many difficulties is naturally very great.

The most important danger we must guard against when we are worried is not taking the path of knowledge pursuit, but succumbing to the environment, being lazy to struggle, seeking temporary peace, until our will declines, we become discouraged, and we follow the crowd until we stop. This is a point that we should pay close attention to, whether we are working hard to improve our personal lives or expanding to reform public undertakings in society.

Finally, we feel that our current worries are mostly about personal prospects, and most of them depend on our own efforts first. Although some people say that these many personal prospects are caused by the current situation of the entire society, the country, and even the whole world, the individual is the foundation of society, a tributary in the ocean of society. If personal problems cannot be adequately resolved by our own efforts first, how can we have the experience, knowledge, and spirit to do greater work to reform society in the future?

Problem Discussion

Why are Shop Assistants Slow to Serve Customers?

— You Ping

The Problem of Shop Assistants Neglecting Customers

Whether people in cities or villages, when they come back from shopping, they are probably always criticizing the poor service of shop assistants. In fact, if we analyze the matter of shop assistants neglecting customers from a fair perspective, we cannot unilaterally blame them. We should consider it a kind of reaction under the current capitalist system. Because the motivation for neglecting customers is partly due to the fact that they have not received high-level education and sufficient self-cultivation. However, the capitalists cannot lightly shirk their responsibility either. Because they do not have the courage and power to resist the high pressure from above, they have no choice but to adopt the method of non-violent resistance, venting their implicit anger on the customers to reduce the store's business.

Originally, any pure young person would want to be an accomplished and respected person. It is only because the environment is too bad that they have to be forced to take the path of being criticized. Driven by life, they abandon school, sell their whole body and mind to the capitalists, and are driven like slaves in order to earn meager salaries to maintain the livelihood of themselves and their families. You think, this is already so pitiful! But the capitalists do not understand, and even more brutally destroy them, arbitrarily extending their working hours, depriving them of the entertainment they should have in life, and preventing them from improving their personal studies. In addition, the surrounding snobs look down on them with contempt, which makes them fundamentally doubt the meaning of life, and feel that the world is unpredictable, as if they are in a society that is both cruel and lacks compassion. Because of this concept infiltrating their minds, a sense of injustice arises in their hearts and is manifested on their faces, and finally creates the so-called "neglecting customers" incident.

Therefore, I dare to assert that if we want to completely change the attitude of shop assistants, we must raise their salaries, transform their environment, revitalize their lives, and enrich their personality. Otherwise, any criticism or sarcasm will absolutely not change their abnormal psychology. However, under the existing social system, how easy is it to transform it?

Life in the Business World

An Experiment in Improving Leisure Life

— Ms. Ouyang Jinping

(Volunteer Teacher in a Shop)

Two or three years ago, my uncle was in Hangzhou, preparing to open a small-scale tea shop. The shop employed a total of seventeen or eight employees, of which apprentices accounted for two-thirds. Speaking of these dozen or so apprentices, they were all from poor backgrounds and had only read two or three elementary school Chinese textbooks, which could be considered to have some basic literacy. Although their jobs were low, several of them were ambitious and hoped to improve themselves. Because they wanted to study but had no money for tuition, after work at 7 o'clock every day, they only had a copy of the newspaper and read a few simple news reports. Sometimes, they were fascinated and read aloud while watching. However, due to their low level, the reading inevitably contained many mistakes. My uncle found it amusing to hear them mispronounce words, such as "He Ying Ci (misreading of the character 'Qin') arrived in Hankou!" "Neng (misreading of the character 'Xiong') Shihui appointed Garrison (misreading of the character 'Shu') Commander!" Therefore, my uncle's motivation to organize a night school arose. One day, he said to the apprentices, "Your level of reading newspapers is not up to par yet, but would you like to concentrate on tutoring? I am willing to sacrifice two hours every day to fulfill a little bit of guidance. However, you must have perseverance!" No one objected at the time. My uncle was also pleased to see their eagerness to learn. Because the shop was not large and the goods were crowded, he rented a small room next to the shop as a classroom. He also allocated a portion of the profits from the surplus as rent. These profits were willingly sacrificed and used by the shop employees. From then on, they had classes every night, and within two years, they had completed the elementary school curriculum. Now, every apprentice has the knowledge of junior high school. The pronunciation is certainly much more accurate than before; when it comes to abacus and written calculations, they are also skilled. Although my uncle is not a great scholar who patiently teaches, he cannot talk about any honor. However, at least he has won the apprentices' warm gratitude, and they often want to find a way to repay him. And the only way to repay is: for all the big and small shop affairs during the day, they all work harder, washing away the bad habit of ordinary shops of being idle after eating their fill!

I believe that Shanghai is a commercial port, and the low-level employees of several self-proclaimed large companies and shops may not have sufficient knowledge. Have the managers prepared any remedies for them? Undoubtedly, they themselves are tied up with official duties and have no time to take on teaching duties. However, at least they should hire an experienced teacher to teach the employees ordinary skills. As the English proverb says: "With sufficient commercial knowledge, there will be sufficient commercial development!" Shop owners, please implement it quickly!

Literary Works

Taking Advantage

— Ying Hui

The incident happened in the workshop. At that time, I was doing the sweeping work, a small worker in the cloth machine room of the ×× yarn factory. There were so many young women in the factory, several hundred. Right where I was sweeping, there was a very beautiful young woman, only sixteen years old. She had been working in the factory for only two weeks. Some people called her the factory flower. I didn't understand what "factory flower" meant at first, but later I learned that it was because her appearance was considered the most beautiful in the whole factory. Speaking of beauty, it was precisely because of her beauty that this happened. The rice buckets, the foreman, big and small, were always staring at her with red eyes. When I saw this situation, I got angry, and the way they looked became more and more disgusting, as if they wanted to swallow her alive.

Her name was Zhang Hongdi, and her number was sixty-two.

I could see that something was not right. Just as expected, I soon discovered that the foreman was flirting with her. The three rice buckets wanted to, but their position was lower than the foreman, so they didn't dare to offend him and let him do it alone. I had seen it coming all along. Sure enough, half an hour before the end of work, he actually started to flirt with Zhang Hongdi. Before, I couldn't catch him doing anything wrong, but this time I clearly heard him say those shameless words: "Little sister, are you tired?"

He put on a smiling face, showing his concern. The little sister ignored him and kept working.

"Sixty-two, are you deaf?" he said again, but the little sister still ignored him. Good, I admired her in my heart. But, I hated the foreman to death and cursed in my heart: "What a decent bastard!" Really, he was forty years old, and the little sister was only sixteen. God knows what was going on. To put it bluntly, she was even younger than his granddaughter. I was angry. He was simply not human, I wasn't wronging him. People ignored him, but he still went forward, saying: "Don't talk, hum, what are you pretending for?"

But good little sister, he was given the cold shoulder again, I was really happy. "After work, let's hang out, okay?"

How about that, that's exactly what it was! He really had the audacity of heaven. I couldn't wait to punch him so that he would fall flat on his back, and say to him: "Do you dare to do it again?" He was not human, he was even worse than a beast. Could people or animals tolerate him?

"Don't be shy, it doesn't matter," he said again. It was simply deceiving the heavens. What kind of talk was that! Alas! The factory was really not a place for people to go. A good woman was easily taken advantage of by bad people as soon as she started working. The foreman, he was so heinous!

"Go away!" I heard this sentence from the little sister was very decisive and powerful. Her face was full of anger. Sixteen years old, she was just a child, how could she stand this? I saw that her eyes were a little red. I was sad, and I thought, I wonder what bad things the previous generation did that required her to suffer such a crime! I don't know if her parents are still alive? If she has parents, and they know that their child is being bullied, what should they do?······ Thinking of this, the foreman turned and walked to the side, and I put this matter down and continued to sweep the floor with a stomach full of anger. For this half day, I stopped working involuntarily. Fortunately, God blessed me and didn't let the rice bucket see me stop working, otherwise, I would probably be fined two yuan, at least two yuan. But how can I eliminate the anger in my stomach? And why should I be angry for others, meddling in other people's business? Forget it. No, I can't forget it, it's just squatting in my stomach and rolling back and forth.

Before long, it was the end of work, which was a relief for me. God, I should have calmed down. No, things are not like that at all. Picking up the lunch box and walking downstairs, I had to hide behind Hongdi for a section of the road. It seemed that I knew something was going to happen.

But things were really coincidental!! After leaving the factory gate, I turned a corner and saw the foreman standing in an alley in the distance. Ah, good thing, he was waiting here, and he must have had ill intentions in his heart. I wanted to see, see what was going on. So I found a place to hide and peek. The other workers were walking home in groups. This matter seemed to be sucking me in, and my legs just couldn't move. The anger in my heart grew even bigger, and the anger was bursting out. At this time, I guessed that things would not end well after all. Alas ! Little sister is so pitiful! Does she have to be bullied because she has a good appearance? Why doesn't God give her an ugly face? Sixteen years old, a girl who is only sixteen years old, how will she live in the future? It's a pity that the little sister has no companions and is walking alone. It's dangerous! What to do? I was anxious for her. Sure enough, the foreman blocked her way. He knew what to say

Page 21

I ran behind him in a few steps. He said, "Little sister, let's go out and have some fun."

"I'm not going!" The little sister said and wanted to walk forward, but he grabbed her hand.

"Little girl, I insist that you go if you don't want to!" He frightened her and dragged her away. The little sister tried to pull away. But she couldn't pull away. At this time, could I still stand by? No, I had to find a way to help her get out of trouble! I clenched my fist, really wanted to jump over and slap him, and then, regardless of the consequences, beat him half to death! But then I thought, no, this would stop my work! What if I was fired, and had to suffer again! I couldn't think anymore, he was dragging her so urgently. "Taking advantage! Taking advantage! Taking advantage!" I was so anxious that I couldn't think of a way, so I shouted three times in a row. There were still many workers on the street, and they immediately saw this incident and ran over, watched, and tightly surrounded the two people. People, layer upon layer, were airtightly surrounded. I was also one of them. This time the foreman let go of his hand. The little sister cried, and people asked her in a chaotic manner. She told everyone about the foreman taking advantage of her, crying and weeping. After she finished speaking, she didn't seem to know what to do.

"You motherfucker!" I heard such a sentence, and then something flew in from behind. I saw blood on the foreman's face. I didn't see what hit him, and no one cared about that. They just watched the foreman in pain and felt happy. At this time, the foreman didn't know what to do either. He couldn't escape, couldn't stand up, and held his hand on the bleeding area of his face.

"Beat him to death!"

"Oppose taking advantage!"

Someone shouted like this. At this time, he couldn't say a word, and his body was shaking a little. Someone really did it. Three young men jumped into the crowd, "slap slap" beat him up, and heard him say "ouch, ouch" a few times and lay down on the ground. Things got big. The three people squeezed out of the crowd after beating him. They were gone, couldn't find their shadows. But the crowd still didn't disperse and was still watching the excitement. Then came a sound of car horns, and a police car drove over from a distance. The car stopped in front of the crowd, and three Chinese police officers came down. People automatically parted a path and let them walk into the circle. The little sister had stopped crying a long time ago,

At this time, she was telling the police about her things. I watched what they were going to do. Later, the two people went to the police station together in the car. Someone served the foreman when he got into the car. He was moaning. I felt a sigh of relief when I saw this. After all, evil people have evil rewards, and the foreman will not be good. I felt happy to beat him. I said that I didn't mean to cover the foreman's eggs. I couldn't really get over it without shouting for a while! A shout caused this big thing! It's good, it's considered to have saved Zhang Hongdi. The foreman and rice buckets usually always bullied others. It's really not okay not to teach them a lesson! In the future, you have to be more careful when taking advantage.

The sixty-two little sister came to work again the next day. But the foreman was injured and detained, so the factory stopped his business.

Self-Employment Introduction

Starting Over

— Ms. Qin

Because of my family's poverty, in the year I graduated from elementary school, I knew that my strength was weak, and I did not dare to harbor any extravagant hopes of entering university. I decided to enter a vocational high school, preparing to find a suitable job in society in the future to solve the problem of livelihood.

Sure enough, I graduated from vocational high school and found a job. However, under the influence of the Shanghai War, unfortunately, the company I served was also lost in the war zone, and I had no choice but to return to my hometown. How miserable! I don't know how many people have been given the gift of the imperialist aggressors' policies!

Later, the ceasefire agreement was signed, and the prosperity of Shanghai gradually recovered. Although the bloodstains of Songhu had not yet dried, I am afraid that the shocking impression of a few months ago was only lingering in the minds of a few people. I, who had been unemployed for several months, had almost gone to the point of desperation step by step. So I could only start over and come to the sea again.

After suffering great emotional stress, I found a place to eat. Although I felt that what I had learned was not being used, I was forced by the problem of bread, so what could I do but "force myself to do it"?

I have been working for half a year now. Not to mention the salary, just in terms of the position I hold, I only feel it is boring and unconscious. A person cannot do well in things that they are not interested in. So I want to find a job that suits me.

What I would like to do is Chinese and English typing or secretarial work. Based on my past experience, I am confident that I can be competent in the above two items. However, because I lack an introduction, I have no choice but to learn from Mao Sui's self-recommendation, and ask your publication to give me an opportunity to disclose. At the same time, if any foreign or local companies or other institutions that need this kind of talent send a letter, I hope you will notify me at any time, and I will be very grateful.

Shop Assistant Communication

Do We Recognize the Puppet State?

To the esteemed Editor,

I am a trainee at a money shop. Recently, I discovered a serious incident in my duties, namely that the drafts entrusted by customers to be sent to the three northeastern provinces are all printed with the words "Year 1 of Datong, Month XX, Day XX" and affixed with the "Great Manchurian State" stamp tax. My colleagues do not pay attention to this and continue to receive and pay as usual. I believe that when the puppet state was established, the people of the country ran around and called for its denial. The righteous army fought bloody battles to recover the lost land. Our country's representatives attending the League of Nations, as well as the countries of the world that uphold justice, expressed their grand theories, hoping that the country would be overthrown. However, the financial institutions in our country, which occupy an important position in the international market, turn a blind eye to it, as if they have tacitly approved it, which is ridiculous! This shows the people of our country's negligence in the matter. Furthermore, if disputes arise with these bills in the future, I believe that the court will also refuse to accept them. I ask for your wise opinion as to whether this is the case. I originally intended to present this situation to the Money Industry Committee, but I am afraid that my words are of little consequence and may not be moving. Therefore, I have no choice but to ask your publication to give me a corner to publish it to the public, hoping that all circles will pay attention to it, and I beg you to send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Money Industry Association to take measures to ban it, as necessary. Sincerely, Hu Ruian

Editor's Note: Since the September 18th Incident occurred last year, everyone knows that our country and nation have reached the most dangerous juncture. If we do not work hard to fight, we can only sit and wait for death. However, what has been the effect in the past fifteen months? It is nothing more than the gradual loss of territory, the successive loss of fortresses, the market is full of inferior goods, and cash is flowing to the east. What is this phenomenon? We can't bear to say it!

Although the livers and brains of most of our compatriots in the three northeastern provinces have been turned into dust under the iron hooves of the slaves! The prosperous streets of Zhabei have been turned into the ashes of the Japanese slaves' artillery fire!·······Alas! What do these, these count for? How can they awaken the delusion of those who only seek profit!

This is not us talking nonsense in the house. The short letter from Mr. Hu above is an excellent proof. We do not want to say much about this matter (and we can't bear to talk about it in detail). We earnestly hope that all money shops in this city will pay special attention to it. At the same time, we hope that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Money Industry Association will have a thorough solution.

The Sea Magazine says: Deer antler is a kind of thing. The world praises the northeast, but the method of production in the north is better. The quality is really not as good as the thickest produced in the west. Others, such as those produced in Jing County, Huguang, are slightly inferior. Those produced in Danshan, Hainan, without branches, are also inferior. A kind of sand deer produced in freshwater places overseas is transformed by sharks. Its color is dry and white and large. There are many branches, and it cannot be used for velvet. This is the worst. Others, such as Fujian, Shaanxi, and Quzhou, all produce it. All can be used for velvet. Change the name to Daodi. Those produced in Japan are called foreign velvet. It is the worst. Not used for medicinal purposes.

Medical Consultant

Outside submissions for medical questions, those disclosed in this publication, will be charged. Those requesting direct replies by letter, must attach a two-cent stamp. Medical Advisory Department

Nocturnal Emission

Wei Yanhe wrote to ask: I have suffered from nocturnal emission for two years. It occurs and heals from time to time. After falling asleep, my ears ring and I have headaches. My spirit is very tired. If I work for too long, I feel even more tired. My memory is weak. I have taken various drugs to stop nocturnal emission, but they have had little effect. I think there must be many patients with this disease. I dare to ask your agency to indicate the cause and treatment. Not only will I benefit, but patients with the same disease will also be grateful.

Answer: The disease of nocturnal emission is indeed a common disease among young people. There are many who have asked this publication. Here is a general answer for the patients' attention.

During the period of male puberty, the semen in the testicles gradually becomes abundant. When the fluid is full, it overflows. The Inner Canon says, "A man is sixteen years old and his kidney qi is strong. The essence qi overflows." Therefore, occasional nocturnal emission is not a disease. It is really because the essence qi is strong and the bone overflows. It is not a disease. Nowadays, men often have nocturnal emission once a month, thinking that this is a serious symptom of nocturnal emission. If they linger for a long time, they will definitely become consumptive. They send letters to inquire, unaware that the fluid overflows when it is full, and has absolutely no bearing on the body. If there are two or three or four or five nocturnal emissions in a month, or even one every other day, then this is truly what is called nocturnal emission. According to recent inquiries, seven or eight out of ten cases of nocturnal emission are mostly caused by masturbation. When a man reaches puberty, his pursuit of all thoughts is occasionally biased, and he is prone to this disease. When he first suffers from it, a young man with a strong body does not feel any pain. Over time, it becomes a habit. Some people even cannot fall asleep without masturbating once a day. They do not know that it is more harmful to their body and depletes their fluids. After a long time, even if they realize it, they have already suffered from the painful disease of nocturnal emission. After masturbating for a long time, the essence gate gradually becomes weak, and the yin fluid is deficient, and the fire of the minister is easily exuberant. Therefore, even if they realize it and can repent and correct their mistakes, they still have nocturnal emission from time to time. Is it not painful? However, there are also those who have nocturnal emission due to excessive use of the brain and the heart fire falling into the kidneys. Although there are occasional cases in the disease inquiry letters, there are not many. The above symptoms, for those who have nocturnal emission due to masturbation, take eight-flavor Rehmannia pill three qian with salt water every morning. For those who have nocturnal emission due to the heart fire falling into the kidneys, take six-flavor Rehmannia pill three qian with boiled water every day. If there is one nocturnal emission per month, this is called overflowing essence and does not require medication. There are still others with or without dreams, which is due to the different pathological roots of the heart and kidneys. Due to limited space, I cannot answer them one by one. I will write a special article to explain them in detail.

Hernia

Chen Chuqing wrote to ask: My right testicle is swollen and large. It has been like this for many days. It can shrink when I sleep. It can also shrink when I press it with my hand. I have taken small intestine hernia pills, but they have no effect. Please tell me how to treat it. Briefly answer: The swelling and enlargement of the right testicle without pain is caused by insufficient middle qi and damp-heat flowing downwards. Here is a pill formula for you: Jisheng orange seed pill, take three qian with boiled water each time.

Small Tidbits of Knowledge

▲Bad Breath

The disease of bad breath. Is particularly troublesome in social situations. Often, in gatherings of distinguished guests where conversations flow freely, even if one's politeness and words are perfectly appropriate, a peculiar odor subtly emanates, inevitably causing others to frown. The cause of this ailment is often due to unresolved heat accumulation in the stomach and intestines, rising liver fire, and constipation. Taking one qian of Angelica and Aloe Pill with salt water every morning allows the accumulated heat to descend, leading to recovery.

▲Acne

Many women suffer from acne due to applying lead-based powder. Rubbing with Cuscuta seed juice will cure it.

▲Acid Reflux

Vomiting after eating, with hidden pain in the stomach. After years of treatment, various medications prove ineffective. Consuming fresh lychees is remarkably effective. If fresh lychees are unavailable, dried lychees can also be used.

Collected Talks on Blood Diseases

Common Knowledge of Blood Disorders (5)

— Ding, Ji, Hua

Coughing Blood

The lung governs Qi. Coughing is a disease of the Qi aspect, hence it belongs to the lung. The lung also manages respiration and externally connects to the skin and hair. External attack of wind and cold causes the skin and hair to close tightly, preventing the lung Qi from flowing smoothly. Internal brewing of heat rises and stimulates. The lung resides at the peak of the five organs, suffering excessive punishment from heat. The blood vessels suddenly rupture, therefore those who cough severely may occasionally see blood. This is heat forcing the blood out, caused by wind and cold invading and the Qi mechanism not flowing. This is what Zhongjing referred to as "coughing with audible panting, severely leading to vomiting blood."

Those with warm, hot, damp and summerheat illnesses can also cough blood because of it. The symptoms are headache, fever, dry mouth, and difficulty urinating, similar to an external contraction of wind and cold. However, this disease is caused by turbid evils entering through the mouth and nose, infiltrating the channels, accumulating between the membranes of the stomach and intestines. The heat stimulates the vessels to rupture, and blood spills from the back into the stomach. The stomach is the place where phlegm is produced. The phlegm goes up with the cough, leading to coughing blood. This is different from the cough caused by wind and cold attacking the skin and then entering the internal organs. These cannot be discussed in the same breath.

For those who cough blood with prolonged coughing and shortness of breath, the lung is shaken by the prolonged coughing, causing Qi to rise upwards in urgency. When Qi rebels, it ignites the fire of the various meridians and the blood of the chest and back channels. Being shaken, the blood comes out with the cough. This condition is often seen in elderly people with prolonged coughs, and is especially severe in cold weather. Because the winter climate is cold. The cough root originates from the lungs receiving cold. Normally, due to climate regulation, the disease symptoms can still be supported. However, upon encountering cold weather, the cold inhaled into the lungs combines with the old disease, making the illness more serious. In winter, the skin and hair are tightly closed, and most breathing is done through the mouth and nose. The cold inhaled through the mouth and nose directly affects the lungs first. Therefore, the disease becomes more severe. It is difficult to estimate the number of older people with Qi rebellion and prolonged coughing who cough blood that is discovered in winter. This condition is most easily mistaken for external contraction coughing blood. If doctors mistreat it, it often leads to consumption and tuberculosis. Be careful, be careful.
